  .linkify {
    display: inline;

  }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





"Read Later" feature in Reading List generates a distilled HTML file for offline reading.



<span class="line"><!---->"Read Later" feature in Reading List generates a distilled HTML file for offline reading.<!----></span>



<br>





Then, the distilled page strips all Content-Security-Policy rules of the original page.



<span class="line"><!---->Then, the distilled page strips all Content-Security-Policy rules of the original page.<!----></span>



<br>





So, if a page prohibits inline script by CSP, attacker can execute it on the distilled HTML that works on the same origin as the original page.



<span class="line"><!---->So, if a page prohibits inline script by CSP, attacker can execute it on the distilled HTML that works on the same origin as the original page.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: 88.0.4324.69+beta



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: 88.0.4324.69+beta<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: iPhone 8 Simulator with iOS 14.3



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: iPhone 8 Simulator with iOS 14.3<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





1) Visit: 



<span class="line"><!---->1) Visit: <!----></span>





https://csrf.jp/2021/chromium_ios/csp-bypass-by-offline.php



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://csrf.jp/2021/chromium_ios/csp-bypass-by-offline.php"><!---->https://csrf.jp/2021/chromium_ios/csp-bypass-by-offline.php<!----></a>



<br>





This page is protected by `Content-Security-Policy: default-src 'self'`



<span class="line"><!---->This page is protected by `Content-Security-Policy: default-src 'self'`<!----></span>



<br>





2) Tap "Read Later" in the Chromium's bottom menu (then the distilled HTML is generated in the background)



<span class="line"><!---->2) Tap "Read Later" in the Chromium's bottom menu (then the distilled HTML is generated in the background)<!----></span>



<br>





3) Open "Reading List"



<span class="line"><!---->3) Open "Reading List"<!----></span>



<br>





4) Long tap the page 1) in the list and choose "Open Offline Version"



<span class="line"><!---->4) Long tap the page 1) in the list and choose "Open Offline Version"<!----></span>



<br>





5) The distilled page is displayed on a tab



<span class="line"><!---->5) The distilled page is displayed on a tab<!----></span>



<br>





6) Tap a hyper-link "SUPPOSE XSS IS HERE" in the page



<span class="line"><!---->6) Tap a hyper-link "SUPPOSE XSS IS HERE" in the page<!----></span>



<br>





7) An alert dialog with cookie values of csrf.jp is shown (i.e., original page's CSP was bypassed)



<span class="line"><!---->7) An alert dialog with cookie values of csrf.jp is shown (i.e., original page's CSP was bypassed)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





CREDIT INFORMATION



<b class="line"><!---->CREDIT INFORMATION<!----></b>



<br>





Muneaki Nishimura (nishimunea)



<span class="line"><!---->Muneaki Nishimura (nishimunea)<!----></span>

FYI: The non-IOS version of this: 



<span class="line"><!---->FYI: The non-IOS version of this: <!----></span>





issue 1012956



<span class="line"><!---->issue 1012956<!----></span>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>





(filled by creis@)



<span class="line"><!---->(filled by creis@)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I don't know about the IOS version. For the non-IOS, the distilled page is running within its own opaque origin, so it won't make any action on behalf of the original document. Risk are mainly about finding a bug in the distiller to execute javascript. You can also potentially be able to exfiltrate data when loading <img> that you weren't able before the distillation.



<span class="line"><!---->I don't know about the IOS version. For the non-IOS, the distilled page is running within its own opaque origin, so it won't make any action on behalf of the original document. Risk are mainly about finding a bug in the distiller to execute javascript. You can also potentially be able to exfiltrate data when loading &lt;img&gt; that you weren't able before the distillation.<!----></span>

The issue of the CSP policy being relaxed in the case of JavaScript is fixed in 1111239. However it is true that on iOS distilled pages do not get a different opaque origin so overall the CSP policy for the original domain is being changed on the distilled page.  Not sure if that warrants any further changes however.



<span class="line"><!---->The issue of the CSP policy being relaxed in the case of JavaScript is fixed in 1111239. However it is true that on iOS distilled pages do not get a different opaque origin so overall the CSP policy for the original domain is being changed on the distilled page.  Not sure if that warrants any further changes however.<!----></span>

Block online content from offline pages



<span class="line"><!---->Block online content from offline pages<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This CL



<span class="line"><!---->This CL<!----></span>



<br>





- moves the offline content in a chrome://offline domain.



<span class="line"><!---->- moves the offline content in a chrome://offline domain.<!----></span>



<br>





- adds content rules to block online resources from chrome://, file://



<span class="line"><!---->- adds content rules to block online resources from chrome://, file://<!----></span>



<br>





  and chrome-distiller:// URLs



<span class="line"><!---->  and chrome-distiller:// URLs<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>
